๐งฉ 1๏ธโฃ backend/api/items.routes.ts (ุชูุณุนุฉ โ endpoint ุฅูุดุงุก ููุชุฌ ุฌุฏูุฏ)
// backend/src/routes/items.routes.ts
import { Router } from 'express';
import { prisma } from '../app';

const r = Router();

// ุงูุจุญุซ ุนุจุฑ EAN (ููุฌูุฏ ูุณุจูุงู)
r.post('/intake-by-ean', async (req, res) => {
  const { ean } = req.body;
  if (!ean) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'EAN missing' });
  const item = await prisma.item.findUnique({ where: { ean } });
  return res.json({ item });
});

// ๐น ุฅูุดุงุก ููุชุฌ ุฌุฏูุฏ ูู Full Form
r.post('/create', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const { name, basePrice, vatRate, hsCode, originCountry, companyId } = req.body;
    if (!name) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Name required' });

    const item = await prisma.item.create({
      data: {
        ean: req.body.ean || `AUTO-${Date.now()}`,
        name,
        basePrice: Number(basePrice || 0),
        vatRate: Number(vatRate || 0),
        hsCode: hsCode || null,
        originCountry: originCountry || 'NL',
        companyId: companyId || null,
      },
    });

    res.json({ ok: true, item });
  } catch (e) {
    console.error(e);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Item create failed', details: String(e) });
  }
});

export default r;
โ๏ธ 2๏ธโฃ backend/app.ts (ุฑุจุท ุงููุณุงุฑ ุงูุฌุฏูุฏ)
// backend/src/app.ts
import express from 'express';
import cors from 'cors';
import bodyParser from 'body-parser';
import { PrismaClient } from '@prisma/client';
import itemsRouter from './routes/items.routes';
import invoicesRouter from './routes/invoices.routes';

const app = express();
app.use(cors());
app.use(bodyParser.json());

export const prisma = new PrismaClient();

app.use('/api/items', itemsRouter);
app.use('/api/invoices', invoicesRouter);

const port = process.env.PORT || 3001;
app.listen(port, () => console.log(`[SBIC] backend running on :${port}`));

// VAT ุงูุชููุงุฆู ุญุณุจ ุงูุจูุฏ
const getDefaultVat = (country: string): number => {
  switch (country) {
    case 'DE': return 19;
    case 'NL': return 21;
    case 'BE': return 21;
    default: return 0; // ุตุงุฏุฑุงุช ุฃู ุฏูู ุฃุฎุฑู
  }
};

// ูู useEffect ุฃู ุนูุฏ ุชุญููู ุงูุตูุญุฉ:
useEffect(() => {
  fetch('/api/company/current').then(res => res.json()).then(data => {
    setCompanyCountry(data?.countryCode || 'NL');
    setVatDefault(getDefaultVat(data?.countryCode || 'NL'));
  });
}, []);

// ุนูุฏ ุญูุธ ุงูููุชุฌ ูู Full Form:
const saveFullFormProduct = async () => {
  if (!ffName) return;
  const body = { name: ffName, basePrice: ffPrice, vatRate: ffVat, hsCode: ffHs, originCountry: ffOrigin, companyId: 'AUTO_COMPANY_FROM_SESSION' };
  const res = await fetch('/api/items/create', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
  });
  const data = await res.json();
  if (data?.item) {
    setLines(prev => [...prev, { description: data.item.name, qty: 1, unit: 'pcs', unitPrice: data.item.basePrice, vat: data.item.vatRate }]);
    setShowFullForm(false);
    setShowEAN(false);
  }
};

model Buyer {
  id           String   @id @default(cuid())
  name         String
  email        String?
  phone        String?
  address      String?
  country      String?   @default("NL")
  vatNumber    String?
  preferredLang String?  @default("en")
  createdAt    DateTime  @default(now())
  updatedAt    DateTime  @updatedAt
  history      BuyerHistory[]
  stats        BuyerStats?
}

model BuyerHistory {
  id        String   @id @default(cuid())
  buyerId   String
  invoiceId String
  amount    Float
  paid      Boolean
  issuedAt  DateTime
}

model BuyerStats {
  id                String   @id @default(cuid())
  buyerId           String   @unique
  totalInvoices     Int      @default(0)
  totalAmount       Float    @default(0)
  averagePaymentDays Int     @default(0)
  lastInvoiceDate   DateTime?
}

๐๏ธ 2๏ธโฃ ุงูุจููุฉ ุงููุงุนุฏูุฉ (Prisma Schema)
model Receipt {
  id           String   @id @default(cuid())
  number       String   @unique
  invoiceId    String
  invoice      Invoice  @relation(fields: [invoiceId], references: [id])
  buyerId      String?
  amount       Float
  paymentDate  DateTime @default(now())
  paymentMethod String  @default("cash")
  currency     String   @default("EUR")
  createdBy    String?
  createdAt    DateTime @default(now())
}
๐งฎ 3๏ธโฃ ุงูู Backend ุงูุฐูู
/api/receipts/auto-generate
import { Router } from 'express';
import { prisma } from '../app';
import PdfPrinter from 'pdfmake';
import fs from 'fs';
import path from 'path';

const r = Router();

r.post('/auto-generate', async (req, res) => {
  const { invoiceId, amount, method = 'cash', user } = req.body;
  const invoice = await prisma.invoice.findUnique({ where: { id: invoiceId }, include: { buyer: true } });
  if (!invoice) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Invoice not found' });

  const count = await prisma.receipt.count();
  const number = `RCPT-${new Date().getFullYear()}-${String(count + 1).padStart(5, '0')}`;

  const receipt = await prisma.receipt.create({
    data: {
      number,
      invoiceId,
      buyerId: invoice.buyerId,
      amount: amount || invoice.totals.total,
      paymentMethod: method,
      createdBy: user || 'system',
    },
  });

  // ุชูููุฏ PDF
  const doc = {
    content: [
      { text: 'CASH RECEIPT VOUCHER', style: 'header' },
      `Receipt No: ${number}`,
      `Invoice No: ${invoice.invoiceNo}`,
      `Customer: ${invoice.buyer?.name || 'N/A'}`,
      `Amount: โฌ${receipt.amount.toFixed(2)}`,
      `Payment Method: ${method}`,
      `Date: ${new Date(receipt.paymentDate).toLocaleDateString()}`,
    ],
    styles: { header: { fontSize: 18, bold: true, alignment: 'center', color: '#C00000' } },
  };

  const printer = new PdfPrinter({ Roboto: { normal: 'node_modules/pdfmake/build/vfs_fonts.js' } });
  const pdfDoc = printer.createPdfKitDocument(doc);
  const file = `/tmp/${number}.pdf`;
  pdfDoc.pipe(fs.createWriteStream(file));
  pdfDoc.end();

  res.json({ ok: true, receipt, file });
});

export default r;

model Invoice {
  id               String   @id @default(cuid())
  invoiceNo        String   @unique
  type             String   @default("sale") // sale | return | draft
  buyerId          String?
  buyer            Buyer?   @relation(fields: [buyerId], references: [id])
  referenceInvoiceId String?  // ุฑุงุจุท ุงููุงุชูุฑุฉ ุงูุฃุตููุฉ
  referenceInvoice   Invoice? @relation("ReturnReference", fields: [referenceInvoiceId], references: [id])
  total             Float
  currency          String   @default("EUR")
  vatTotal          Float    @default(0)
  netTotal          Float    @default(0)
  createdAt         DateTime @default(now())
  updatedAt         DateTime @updatedAt
}

/api/invoices/create-return
r.post('/create-return', async (req, res) => {
  const { originalInvoiceId, items, reason, user } = req.body;

  const original = await prisma.invoice.findUnique({
    where: { id: originalInvoiceId },
    include: { buyer: true },
  });

  if (!original) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Original invoice not found' });

  const count = await prisma.invoice.count({ where: { type: 'return' } });
  const invoiceNo = `RET-${new Date().getFullYear()}-${String(count + 1).padStart(5, '0')}`;

  const total = items.reduce((acc, i) => acc + i.price * i.qty, 0);
  const vatTotal = total * 0.21; // ูููู ุญุณุจ ุจูุฏ ุงูุนููู ูุงุญูุงู
  const netTotal = total + vatTotal;

  const newReturn = await prisma.invoice.create({
    data: {
      invoiceNo,
      type: 'return',
      referenceInvoiceId: originalInvoiceId,
      buyerId: original.buyerId,
      total,
      vatTotal,
      netTotal,
    },
  });

  // ุฅูุดุงุก ุญุฑูุฉ ูุงููุฉ ุนูุณูุฉ
  await prisma.transaction.create({
    data: {
      type: 'credit',
      description: `Return for invoice ${original.invoiceNo}`,
      amount: netTotal,
      buyerId: original.buyerId,
      invoiceId: newReturn.id,
      createdBy: user || 'system',
    },
  });

  res.json({ ok: true, newReturn });
});

model Tenant {
  id           String   @id @default(cuid())
  name         String
  type         String   @default("company") // company | accounting_firm
  country      String?
  ownerId      String   // ุงููุณุชุฎุฏู ุงูุฃุณุงุณู (ุตุงุญุจ ุงูุดุฑูุฉ ุฃู ูุฏูุฑ ุงูููุชุจ)
  companies    Company[]
  users        User[]
  createdAt    DateTime @default(now())
}

model Company {
  id           String   @id @default(cuid())
  tenantId     String
  tenant       Tenant   @relation(fields: [tenantId], references: [id])
  name         String
  country      String
  vatNumber    String?
  currency     String   @default("EUR")
  invoices     Invoice[]
}

model Invoice {
  id           String   @id @default(cuid())
  companyId    String
  company      Company  @relation(fields: [companyId], references: [id])
  buyerId      String?
  buyer        Buyer?   @relation(fields: [buyerId], references: [id])
  total        Float
  vatRate      Float
  vatTotal     Float
  netTotal     Float
  type         String   @default("sale") // sale | return
}

model Tenant {
  id        String   @id @default(cuid())
  name      String
  type      String   @default("company") // company | group | accounting_firm
  country   String?
  ownerId   String
  companies Company[]
  users     User[]
  createdAt DateTime @default(now())
}

model Company {
  id        String   @id @default(cuid())
  tenantId  String
  name      String
  country   String
  vatNumber String?
  currency  String   @default("EUR")
  invoices  Invoice[]
}

model Invoice {
  id          String   @id @default(cuid())
  companyId   String
  type        String   @default("sale") // sale | return
  buyerId     String?
  total       Float
  vatRate     Float
  vatExempt   Boolean  @default(false)
  vatReason   String?
  createdAt   DateTime @default(now())
}

// packages/prisma/schema.prisma

generator client {
  provider = "prisma-client-js"
}

datasource db {
  provider = "postgresql"
  url      = env("DATABASE_URL")
}

model Tenant {
  id        String   @id @default(cuid())
  name      String
  type      String   @default("company") // company | group | accounting_firm
  country   String?
  ownerId   String
  companies Company[]
  users     User[]
  createdAt DateTime @default(now())
}

model Company {
  id        String   @id @default(cuid())
  tenantId  String
  tenant    Tenant   @relation(fields: [tenantId], references: [id])
  name      String
  country   String
  vatNumber String?
  currency  String   @default("EUR")
  buyers    Buyer[]
  invoices  Invoice[]
  receipts  Receipt[]
  createdAt DateTime @default(now())
}

4) ุทุจูุฉ ุงูุฐูุงุก โ ai-core (ูุงุฌูุงุช ุฃูููุฉ)
// packages/ai-core/src/index.ts
export type BuyerContext = { companyCountry: string; buyerCountry?: string; isBusiness?: boolean };

export function suggestVat(ctx: BuyerContext) {
  const { companyCountry, buyerCountry, isBusiness } = ctx;
  if (!buyerCountry || companyCountry === buyerCountry) return { rate: companyCountry === 'DE' ? 19 : 21, exempt: false, reason: null };
  if (isBusiness) return { rate: 0, exempt: true, reason: 'Intra-EU B2B โ Reverse charge.' };
  return { rate: 0, exempt: true, reason: 'Export โ VAT exempt.' };
}

export function awardLoyalty(pointsBase: number, reviewBonus = 50) {
  return {
    invoicePoints: Math.max(0, Math.floor(pointsBase)),
    reviewPoints: reviewBonus,
  };
}

12) ุฃูุซูุฉ ููุฏ โ Hardening
Middleware: Idempotency-Key
// apps/api-gateway/src/mw/idempotency.ts
import type { Request, Response, NextFunction } from 'express';
import { prisma } from '../index';

export async function idempotency(req: Request, res: Response, next: NextFunction) {
  if (!['POST','PUT','PATCH'].includes(req.method)) return next();
  const key = req.header('Idempotency-Key');
  if (!key) return res.status(400).json({ ok:false, error:'Missing Idempotency-Key' });
  const hit = await prisma.auditLog.findFirst({ where: { action:'idem', entity:key } });
  if (hit) return res.status(409).json({ ok:false, error:'Duplicate request' });
  await prisma.auditLog.create({ data: { tenantId: req.header('X-Tenant')||'n/a', actor:'api', action:'idem', entity:key } });
  next();
}
Webhook Verify (HMAC)
// apps/api-gateway/src/mw/webhookVerify.ts
import crypto from 'crypto';
export function verifyWebhook(req, res, next) {
  const sig = req.header('X-Signature')||'';
  const secret = process.env.WEBHOOK_SECRET||'';
  const body = JSON.stringify(req.body);
  const h = crypto.createHmac('sha256', secret).update(body).digest('hex');
  if (sig !== h) return res.status(401).json({ ok:false, error:'Invalid signature' });
  next();
}
Queue Job (BullMQ)
// packages/commerce-core/src/queues.ts
import { Queue } from 'bullmq';
export const syncOrdersQ = new Queue('sync:orders');
export const syncRefundsQ = new Queue('sync:refunds');

model Role {
  id        String   @id @default(cuid())
  tenantId  String
  name      String   // owner | accountant | manager | staff | external
  policies  Policy[]
}

model Policy {
  id        String   @id @default(cuid())
  roleId    String
  role      Role     @relation(fields: [roleId], references: [id])
  scope     String   // invoice:create | vat:update | loyalty:export | *
  effect    String   @default("allow") // allow | deny
}

model AuditLog {
  id        String   @id @default(cuid())
  tenantId  String
  actor     String
  action    String
  entity    String?
  hash      String?
  payload   Json?
  ip        String?
  userAgent String?
  createdAt DateTime @default(now())
}
๐ง 3๏ธโฃ ุงูููุทู ุงูุฃุณุงุณู (RBAC & Auth)
// middleware/auth.ts
import jwt from 'jsonwebtoken';
import { prisma } from '../index';

export async function auth(req, res, next) {
  const token = req.header('Authorization')?.replace('Bearer ', '');
  if (!token) return res.status(401).json({ ok: false, error: 'Missing token' });

  try {
    const decoded = jwt.verify(token, process.env.JWT_SECRET);
    req.user = decoded;
    const { roleId } = decoded;
    const path = `${req.method.toLowerCase()}:${req.path}`;
    const policies = await prisma.policy.findMany({ where: { roleId } });
    const allowed = policies.some(p =>
      path.includes(p.scope.split(':')[0]) && p.effect === 'allow'
    );
    if (!allowed) return res.status(403).json({ ok: false, error: 'Access denied' });
    next();
  } catch (e) {
    res.status(401).json({ ok: false, error: 'Invalid token' });
  }
}
๐งพ 4๏ธโฃ ุงูุญูุงูุฉ ูู ุงูุชูุฑุงุฑ (Idempotency Middleware)
// middleware/idempotency.ts
import { prisma } from '../index';

export async function idempotency(req, res, next) {
  if (!['POST', 'PUT', 'PATCH'].includes(req.method)) return next();
  const key = req.header('Idempotency-Key');
  if (!key) return res.status(400).json({ ok: false, error: 'Missing Idempotency-Key' });

  const hit = await prisma.auditLog.findFirst({ where: { action: 'idem', entity: key } });
  if (hit) return res.status(409).json({ ok: false, error: 'Duplicate request' });

  await prisma.auditLog.create({
    data: { tenantId: req.header('X-Tenant') || 'n/a', actor: req.user?.email || 'api', action: 'idem', entity: key },
  });
  next();
}
๐ก 5๏ธโฃ ุงูุชุญูู ูู Webhooks (HMAC + Timestamp)
// middleware/webhookVerify.ts
import crypto from 'crypto';

export function verifyWebhook(req, res, next) {
  const sig = req.header('X-Signature');
  const ts  = req.header('X-Timestamp');
  const secret = process.env.WEBHOOK_SECRET || '';
  if (!sig || !ts) return res.status(401).json({ ok: false, error: 'Missing headers' });

  const age = Date.now() - Number(ts);
  if (age > 5 * 60 * 1000) return res.status(401).json({ ok: false, error: 'Signature expired' });

  const body = JSON.stringify(req.body);
  const h = crypto.createHmac('sha256', secret).update(ts + '.' + body).digest('hex');
  if (sig !== h) return res.status(401).json({ ok: false, error: 'Invalid signature' });
  next();
}
๐งฎ 6๏ธโฃ ุณุฌู ุงูุชุฏููู ุงูุฐูู (Audit Service)
// services/audit.service.ts
import { prisma } from '../index';
import crypto from 'crypto';

export async function logAudit(tenantId, actor, action, entity, payload) {
  const hash = crypto.createHash('sha256').update(JSON.stringify(payload || {})).digest('hex');
  return prisma.auditLog.create({
    data: { tenantId, actor, action, entity, hash, payload },
  });
}

๐ง 3๏ธโฃ ุงูุฐูุงุก ุงูุชูุจุคู (Forecasting AI Layer)
ูุนุชูุฏ ุนูู:

// ai/forecast.sales.ts
export function forecastSales(data: SaleRecord[], months = 6) {
  const growth = movingAverage(data.map(x => x.amount), 7);
  const trend = growth[growth.length - 1] * (1 + 0.05 * months);
  return {
    forecast: trend,
    confidence: 0.92,
    message: `Expected growth ${(trend / growth[growth.length - 1] - 1) * 100}%`
  };
}

// core/ai.kernel.ts
export async function executeCommand(command) {
  switch (command.action) {
    case 'generate_report':
      return await FiscalModule.generateReport(command.params);
    case 'forecast':
      return await AnalyticsModule.forecast(command.params);
    case 'sync_tenants':
      return await TenantManager.syncAll();
    case 'alert_review':
      return await AlertsModule.notify(command.params);
    default:
      return { status: 'unknown_command' };
  }
}

import { sbic, loyalty, analytics } from './connectors/index.js';

export async function execute(command) {
  const { type, target, params } = command;
  switch (type) {
    case 'report.generate':
      return await sbic.generateReport(params);
    case 'forecast.run':
      return await analytics.forecast(params);
    case 'loyalty.reward':
      return await loyalty.rewardCustomer(params);
    case 'sync.tenants':
      return await orchestrator.syncAll();
    default:
      return { status: 'unknown', message: 'Command not recognized' };
  }
}

GitHub Actions Workflow

name: Deploy to Sovereign Cloud
on:
  push:
    branches: [main]
jobs:
  deploy:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - name: Build & Push Docker Images
        run: |
          docker build -t sorooh/ucc-sep:latest .
          docker push sorooh/ucc-sep:latest
      - name: Deploy to K8s
        uses: azure/k8s-deploy@v5
        with:
          manifests: |
            infra/kubernetes/ucc-sep.yml
          namespace: sorooh

export async function execute(command) {
  const { type, params } = command || {};
  const result = await routeCommand(type, params);
  if (process.env.EXEC_AI_ENABLED === 'true') {
    await axios.post(process.env.EXEC_AI_REPORT_CHANNEL, {
      type, params, result, timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    });
  }
  return result;
}

setInterval(async () => {

    if (alerts?.length) console.log('โ๏ธ Predictive Alerts:', alerts);

๐น 5. ูุญุฏุฉ ุงูุชูุจุค (modules/predictive/index.js)
import { runForecast } from '../analytics/index.js';
import { createAlert } from '../alerts/index.js';

export async function predictiveMonitor() {
  const forecast = await runForecast({ months: 1 });
  const alerts = [];

  if (forecast.revenue_forecast < 120000) {
    alerts.push(await createAlert({ 
      level: 'warning', 
      message: 'Expected revenue below target next month' 
    }));
  }

  if (Math.random() > 0.85) {
    alerts.push(await createAlert({ 
      level: 'critical', 
      message: 'Possible supplier delay detected' 
    }));
  }

  return alerts;
}

FDC_ENABLED=true
FDC_CONFIDENCE_THRESHOLD=0.85

ููู modules/fdc/index.js:

import { sendEmail } from '../alerts/index.js';
import { getLedgerSummary } from '../analytics/index.js';
import { rewardCustomer } from '../loyalty/index.js';

export async function runFDC() {
  const summary = await getLedgerSummary();
  const liquidity = summary.cash / summary.total_assets;
  const alerts = [];

  if (liquidity < 0.25) {
    alerts.push({ level:'critical', message:'Liquidity below 25%' });
    await sendEmail(process.env.FDC_NOTIFY_EMAIL, 'โ๏ธ Low Liquidity', 'Consider halting purchases temporarily.');
  }

  if (summary.profit_margin > 0.3) {
    alerts.push({ level:'info', message:'High Profit Margin โ Consider reinvestment or bonuses' });
    await rewardCustomer({ buyerId:'global', points:500 });
  }

  return alerts;
}
ูููุณุชุฏุนู ูุฐุง ุงููุญุฑู ูู 12 ุณุงุนุฉ:

setInterval(runFDC, 12 * 3600 * 1000);

ุชุณุฌูู ุงููุฑุงุฑ ุงููุงุชุฌ ูู ุฌุฏูู financial_decisions.

๐น 6. ุณุฌูู ุงููุฑุงุฑุงุช ุงููุงููุฉ (Financial Decision Ledger)
CREATE TABLE financial_decisions (
  id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
  company TEXT,
  decision_type TEXT,
  amount NUMERIC(18,2),
  target_company TEXT,
  rationale TEXT,
  confidence NUMERIC(3,2),
  executed BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT now()
);

๐น 4. ุงูุชูููุฐ ุงูุจุฑูุฌู (ุงููุจุฏุฃู)
ูู modules/executive_board/index.js:

import { getCompanyData } from '../analytics/index.js';
import { runFDC } from '../fdc/index.js';
import { runForecast } from '../analytics/index.js';

export async function holdBoardMeeting() {
  const agents = ['S', 'B', 'R', 'M', 'N', 'F'];
  const reports = await Promise.all(
    agents.map(async a => ({ agent: a, data: await getCompanyData(a) }))
  );

  const proposals = reports.map(r => ({
    agent: r.agent,
    proposal: analyzeData(r.data)
  }));

  const decision = reachConsensus(proposals);
  await dispatchDecision(decision);
  return decision;
}

function analyzeData(data) {
  if (data.profit_margin > 0.25) return 'Increase Reinvestment';
  if (data.liquidity < 0.2) return 'Request InterCompany Support';
  return 'Maintain Policy';
}

function reachConsensus(proposals) {
  const votes = {};
  for (const p of proposals) votes[p.proposal] = (votes[p.proposal] || 0) + 1;
  const best = Object.entries(votes).sort((a,b)=>b[1]-a[1])[0][0];
  return { decision: best, votes };
}

async function dispatchDecision(decision) {
  console.log('๐งญ Executive Decision:', decision);
  await runFDC(); // Example follow-up action
}

๐น 3. ูุงุนุฏุฉ ุงูุจูุงูุงุช (financial_tables.sql)
CREATE TABLE financial_records (
  id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
  company TEXT,
  date DATE,
  revenue NUMERIC(12,2),
  expenses NUMERIC(12,2),
  profit NUMERIC(12,2),
  liquidity NUMERIC(12,2),
  risk_score NUMERIC(3,2),
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT now()
);

CREATE TABLE financial_decisions (
  id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
  decision_type TEXT,
  company TEXT,
  reason TEXT,
  confidence NUMERIC(3,2),
  status TEXT DEFAULT 'pending',
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT now()
);
๐น 4. ููุทู ุงููุฑุงุฑุงุช (core/fdc.engine.js)
export async function analyzeFinance(record) {
  const { revenue, expenses, liquidity } = record;
  const profitMargin = (revenue - expenses) / revenue;
  const decisions = [];

  if (liquidity < 0.25) {
    decisions.push({
      type: 'Liquidity Alert',
      reason: 'Liquidity below 25% threshold',
      confidence: 0.92
    });
  }
  if (profitMargin > 0.3) {
    decisions.push({
      type: 'Reinvestment Recommendation',
      reason: 'High profit margin detected',
      confidence: 0.88
    });
  }
  if (profitMargin < 0.1) {
    decisions.push({
      type: 'Expense Review',
      reason: 'Low profit margin below 10%',
      confidence: 0.95
    });
  }
  return decisions;
}
๐น 5. ูุงุฌูุฉ ุงูุจุฑูุฌุฉ (fdc.routes.js)
import express from 'express';
import { analyzeFinance } from '../core/fdc.engine.js';
const router = express.Router();

router.post('/analyze', async (req, res) => {
  const result = await analyzeFinance(req.body);
  res.json({ ok: true, result });
});

export default router;

  id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
  company TEXT,
  date DATE DEFAULT CURRENT_DATE,
  revenue NUMERIC(12,2),
  expenses NUMERIC(12,2),
  liquidity NUMERIC(12,2),
  profit NUMERIC(12,2),
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT now()
);

  id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
  company TEXT,
  decision_type TEXT,
  reason TEXT,
  confidence NUMERIC(3,2),
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT now()
);

export async function analyzeFinance({ revenue, expenses, liquidity }) {
  const profit = revenue - expenses;
  const profitMargin = profit / revenue;
  const decisions = [];

  if (liquidity < 0.25) {
    decisions.push({ type: 'Liquidity Alert', reason: 'Liquidity below 25%', confidence: 0.91 });
  }
  if (profitMargin < 0.1) {
    decisions.push({ type: 'Expense Review', reason: 'Low margin under 10%', confidence: 0.94 });
  }
  if (profitMargin > 0.3) {
    decisions.push({ type: 'Reinvestment', reason: 'High profit margin', confidence: 0.88 });
  }

  return { profit, profitMargin, decisions };
}

  }

import PDFDocument from 'pdfkit';
import fs from 'fs';

export function generateFDCReport({ company, revenue, expenses, profit, liquidity, decisions }) {
  const doc = new PDFDocument();
  const fileName = `./reports/FDC_Report_${company}_${new Date().toISOString().slice(0,7)}.pdf`;
  doc.pipe(fs.createWriteStream(fileName));

  // Header
  doc.fontSize(22).text(`Surooh Financial Decision Report`, { align: 'center' });
  doc.moveDown(1);
  doc.fontSize(14).text(`Company: ${company}`);
  doc.text(`Date: ${new Date().toLocaleDateString()}`);
  doc.moveDown(1);

  // Summary
  doc.fontSize(16).text(`๐ Financial Summary`);
  doc.fontSize(12).text(`Revenue: โฌ${revenue.toFixed(2)}`);
  doc.text(`Expenses: โฌ${expenses.toFixed(2)}`);
  doc.text(`Profit: โฌ${profit.toFixed(2)}`);
  doc.text(`Liquidity Ratio: ${(liquidity * 100).toFixed(1)}%`);
  doc.moveDown(1);

  // Decisions
  doc.fontSize(16).text(`๐ง System Decisions`);
  decisions.forEach((d, i) => {
    doc.fontSize(12).text(`${i + 1}. ${d.type} โ ${d.reason} (Confidence: ${(d.confidence * 100).toFixed(1)}%)`);
  });
  doc.moveDown(1);

  // Footer
  doc.fontSize(10).text(`Generated automatically by Surooh FDC Engine`, { align: 'center' });

  doc.end();
  return fileName;
}
๐น 3. ุชุนุฏูู /routes/fdc.routes.js ูุฅุถุงูุฉ ุชูููุฏ ุงูุชูุฑูุฑ

import { analyzeFinance } from '../core/fdc.engine.js';
import { generateFDCReport } from '../core/fdc.report.js';

const router = express.Router();

router.post('/analyze', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const result = await analyzeFinance(req.body);
    const pdfPath = generateFDCReport({
      company: req.body.company || 'Surooh Holding',
      ...req.body,
      profit: result.profit,
      decisions: result.decisions
    });
    res.json({ ok: true, result, pdf: pdfPath });
  } catch (err) {
    res.status(500).json({ ok: false, error: err.message });
  }
});

export default router;

import nodemailer from 'nodemailer';
import fs from 'fs';

export async function sendFDCReport(email, filePath) {
  const transporter = nodemailer.createTransport({
    service: 'gmail',
    auth: {
      user: process.env.MAIL_USER,
      pass: process.env.MAIL_PASS
    }
  });

  await transporter.sendMail({
    from: `"Surooh Finance" <${process.env.MAIL_USER}>`,
    to: email,
    subject: 'Monthly Financial Decision Report',
    text: 'Attached is your monthly FDC report.',
    attachments: [{ filename: filePath.split('/').pop(), content: fs.createReadStream(filePath) }]
  });

  console.log(`๐ง Report sent to ${email}`);
}

import { analyzeFinance } from './fdc.engine.js';

๐น 1. ูุญุฏุฉ ูุฑุงุกุฉ ุงููููุงุช โ /core/fdc.storage.js
import fs from 'fs';
import path from 'path';

export function listReports() {
  const folder = path.resolve('./reports');
  if (!fs.existsSync(folder)) return [];

  return fs.readdirSync(folder)
    .filter(f => f.endsWith('.pdf'))
    .map(file => ({
      name: file,
      path: `/reports/${file}`,
      company: file.split('_')[2],
      period: file.split('_')[3]?.replace('.pdf', ''),
      created: fs.statSync(path.join(folder, file)).mtime
    }))
    .sort((a, b) => b.created - a.created);
}

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';

export default function FDCDashboard() {
  const [reports, setReports] = useState([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetch('/api/fdc/reports')
      .then(res => res.json())
      .then(data => setReports(data.reports || []));
  }, []);

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-50 p-10">
      <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold text-center mb-8 text-gray-800">
        ๐ Surooh FDC Report Dashboard
      </h1>
      <table className="w-full border-collapse shadow bg-white rounded-xl overflow-hidden">
        <thead className="bg-gray-100 text-left">
          <tr>
            <th className="p-3">ุงูุดุฑูุฉ</th>
            <th className="p-3">ุงููุชุฑุฉ</th>
            <th className="p-3">ุชุงุฑูุฎ ุงูุฅูุดุงุก</th>
            <th className="p-3">ุงูููู</th>
          </tr>
        </thead>
        <tbody>
          {reports.map((r, i) => (
            <tr key={i} className="border-t hover:bg-gray-50">
              <td className="p-3">{r.company}</td>
              <td className="p-3">{r.period || 'ุบูุฑ ูุญุฏุฏุฉ'}</td>
              <td className="p-3">{new Date(r.created).toLocaleString()}</td>
              <td className="p-3">
                <a href={r.path} target="_blank" className="text-red-600 underline">
                  ุชุญููู ุงูุชูุฑูุฑ
                </a>
              </td>
            </tr>

  for (const file of files) {
    // ุงุณุชุฎูุงุต ุงูุดูุฑ ูู ุงูุงุณู

import { sendFDCReport } from './fdc.mail.js';
import { sendTelegramAlert } from './fdc.telegram.js';

export async function checkFinancialStatus(record) {
  const alerts = [];
  const { company, revenue, expenses, liquidity, profit } = record;

  const profitMargin = profit / revenue;
  const expenseRatio = expenses / revenue;

  if (liquidity < 0.25) {
    alerts.push(`๐จ [${company}] ุงูุณูููุฉ ุงูุฎูุถุช ุฅูู ${(liquidity * 100).toFixed(1)}% ููุท!`);
  }
  if (expenseRatio > 0.8) {
    alerts.push(`โ๏ธ [${company}] ุงููุตุฑููุงุช ุชุฌุงูุฒุช 80% ูู ุงูุฅูุฑุงุฏุงุช!`);
  }
  if (profitMargin < 0.1) {
    alerts.push(`โ [${company}] ูุงูุด ุงูุฑุจุญ ุงูุฎูุถ ูุฃูู ูู 10%.`);
  }
  if (profitMargin > 0.4) {
    alerts.push(`๐ [${company}] ุฃุฏุงุก ููุชุงุฒ! ุงูุฑุจุญ ุชุฌุงูุฒ 40%.`);
  }

  for (const msg of alerts) {
    await sendTelegramAlert(msg);
    await sendFDCReport(process.env.ALERT_MAIL, msg);
  }

  return alerts;
}
๐น 2. ูุญุฏุฉ ุงูุชูุบุฑุงู โ /core/fdc.telegram.js
import fetch from 'node-fetch';

export async function sendTelegramAlert(message) {
  const TOKEN = process.env.TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN;
  const CHAT_ID = process.env.TELEGRAM_CHAT_ID;
  if (!TOKEN || !CHAT_ID) return;

  await fetch(`https://api.telegram.org/bot${TOKEN}/sendMessage`, {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify({ chat_id: CHAT_ID, text: message })
  });
}
๐น 3. ุงุฎุชุจุงุฑ ูุฏูู โ /routes/fdc.alerts.js

import { checkFinancialStatus } from '../core/fdc.alerts.js';
const router = express.Router();

router.post('/check', async (req, res) => {
  const alerts = await checkFinancialStatus(req.body);
  res.json({ ok: true, alerts });
});

export default router;

CREATE TABLE invoices (
  id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
  company TEXT,
  date DATE,
  total_amount NUMERIC(12,2),
  expense NUMERIC(12,2) DEFAULT 0,
  status TEXT DEFAULT 'paid'
);
๐น 2. ุฅูุดุงุก ูุงุฌูุฉ API ูู SBIC โ /routes/invoices.routes.js
import express from 'express';
import db from '../db/connect.js';
const router = express.Router();

router.get('/summary/:company', async (req, res) => {
  const { company } = req.params;
  const result = await db.query(`
    SELECT
      SUM(total_amount) AS revenue,
      SUM(expense) AS expenses
    FROM invoices
    WHERE company = $1
      AND date >= date_trunc('month', CURRENT_DATE)
  `, [company]);
  res.json(result.rows[0]);
});

export default router;
๐น 3. ูุญุฏุฉ ุงูุฑุจุท ุฏุงุฎู FDC โ /core/fdc.integration.js
import fetch from 'node-fetch';

export async function fetchSBICData(company) {
  const base = process.env.SBIC_API_URL || 'http://localhost:8081';
  const res = await fetch(`${base}/api/invoices/summary/${company}`);
  const data = await res.json();

  return {
    company,
    revenue: parseFloat(data.revenue || 0),
    expenses: parseFloat(data.expenses || 0),
    liquidity: (Math.random() * 0.4 + 0.2).toFixed(2), // ูุคูุชูุง ุญุชู ูุฑุจุท ูุน ุงูุญุณุงุจ ุงูุจููู
    profit: data.revenue - data.expenses
  };
}
๐น 4. ุชุนุฏูู ุงูุฌุฏููุฉ ุงูุดูุฑูุฉ โ /core/fdc.scheduler.js
import { fetchSBICData } from './fdc.integration.js';
import { analyzeFinance } from './fdc.engine.js';
import { generateFDCReport } from './fdc.report.js';

const companies = ['Surooh Holding', 'Borvat', 'Royal International'];

cron.schedule('0 8 1 * *', async () => {
  console.log('๐ Running integrated FDC report job...');

  for (const c of companies) {
    const record = await fetchSBICData(c);
    const result = await analyzeFinance(record);
    const pdf = generateFDCReport({ ...record, decisions: result.decisions });
    console.log(`โ Report generated for ${c}: ${pdf}`);
  }
});

import fetch from 'node-fetch';

// ูุซุงู ุงุชุตุงู ุนุงู โ ูุงุญูุงู ููุฎุตุต ููู ุจูู (ING, ABN AMRO, Deutsche Bank, etc.)
export async function fetchBankTransactions(company) {
  const BANK_API_URL = process.env.BANK_API_URL;
  const TOKEN = process.env.BANK_API_TOKEN;

  const res = await fetch(`${BANK_API_URL}/transactions?company=${encodeURIComponent(company)}`, {
    headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${TOKEN}` }
  });

  if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Bank API error for ${company}`);
  const data = await res.json();

  return data.transactions.map(tx => ({
    date: tx.date,
    amount: parseFloat(tx.amount),
    type: tx.amount > 0 ? 'in' : 'out',
    description: tx.description
  }));
}
๐น 2. ูุญุฏุฉ ุงูุชุญููู ุงูููุฏู โ /core/fdc.cashflow.js
export function analyzeCashFlow(transactions) {
  const totalIn = transactions.filter(t => t.type === 'in').reduce((a, b) => a + b.amount, 0);
  const totalOut = transactions.filter(t => t.type === 'out').reduce((a, b) => a + Math.abs(b.amount), 0);
  const netFlow = totalIn - totalOut;
  const liquidity = totalIn > 0 ? (netFlow / totalIn).toFixed(2) : 0;

  return {
    totalIn,
    totalOut,
    netFlow,
    liquidity,
    riskLevel:
      liquidity < 0.2 ? 'High Risk' :
      liquidity < 0.4 ? 'Moderate Risk' : 'Stable'
  };
}
๐น 3. ูุงุฌูุฉ ุงุฎุชุจุงุฑ ูุฏููุฉ โ /routes/fdc.bank.routes.js
import express from 'express';
import { fetchBankTransactions } from '../core/fdc.bank.js';
import { analyzeCashFlow } from '../core/fdc.cashflow.js';
const router = express.Router();

router.get('/cashflow/:company', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const transactions = await fetchBankTransactions(req.params.company);
    const summary = analyzeCashFlow(transactions);
    res.json({ ok: true, summary, transactions });
  } catch (e) {
    res.status(500).json({ ok: false, error: e.message });
  }
});

export default router;

๐น 1. ูุญุฏุฉ ุงูุฏูุฌ ุงูุฎูููุฉ โ /core/uld.aggregator.js
import { fetchSBICData } from './fdc.integration.js';
import { fetchBankTransactions } from './fdc.bank.js';
import { analyzeCashFlow } from './fdc.cashflow.js';
import { analyzeFinance } from './fdc.engine.js';

export async function getUnifiedLiquidity(company) {
  const sbic = await fetchSBICData(company);
  const txs = await fetchBankTransactions(company);
  const cash = analyzeCashFlow(txs);
  const finance = await analyzeFinance(sbic);

  const balanceHealth =
    cash.liquidity < 0.2 ? '๐ด ุฎุทุฑ ุนุงูู' :
    cash.liquidity < 0.4 ? '๐ ูุชูุณุท' : '๐ข ูุณุชูุฑ';

  return {
    company,
    revenue: sbic.revenue,
    expenses: sbic.expenses,
    profit: finance.profit,
    liquidityRatio: cash.liquidity,
    netCashFlow: cash.netFlow,
    riskLevel: balanceHealth,
    updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
  };
}
๐น 2. ูุงุฌูุฉ API โ /routes/uld.routes.js
import express from 'express';
import { getUnifiedLiquidity } from '../core/uld.aggregator.js';
const router = express.Router();

const companies = ['Surooh Holding', 'Borvat', 'Royal International'];

router.get('/', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const reports = [];
    for (const c of companies) {
      const summary = await getUnifiedLiquidity(c);
      reports.push(summary);
    }
    res.json({ ok: true, reports });
  } catch (err) {
    res.status(500).json({ ok: false, error: err.message });
  }
});

export default router;

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';

export default function ULDDashboard() {
  const [data, setData] = useState([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetch('/api/uld')
      .then(res => res.json())
      .then(d => setData(d.reports || []));
  }, []);

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-50 p-8">
      <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold text-center mb-8 text-gray-800">
        ๐ง Unified Liquidity Dashboard
      </h1>

      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
        {data.map((item, i) => (
          <div key={i} className="bg-white rounded-xl shadow-md p-6 hover:shadow-lg transition">
            <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold text-gray-700 mb-3">{item.company}</h2>
            <p>๐ ุงูุฅูุฑุงุฏุงุช: โฌ{item.revenue.toLocaleString()}</p>
            <p>๐ธ ุงููุตุฑููุงุช: โฌ{item.expenses.toLocaleString()}</p>
            <p>๐ฐ ุงูุฑุจุญ ุงูุตุงูู: โฌ{item.profit.toLocaleString()}</p>
            <p>๐ง ุงูุณูููุฉ: {(item.liquidityRatio * 100).toFixed(1)}%</p>
            <p>๐ ุงูุชุฏูู ุงูููุฏู: โฌ{item.netCashFlow.toLocaleString()}</p>
            <p className="mt-2 font-medium">{item.riskLevel}</p>
            <p className="text-xs text-gray-400 mt-2">ุชุญุฏูุซ: {new Date(item.updatedAt).toLocaleString()}</p>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
๐น 4. ุงููุธูุฑ ุงูุนุงู
ุชุตููู ุฃุจูุถ ุฑูุงุฏู ูุน ููุณุฉ ุญูุฑุงุก (ูููุฉ SBIC).
